FADD \$X, \$Y, \$Z \char`\"{}\+Floating add\char`\"{}. 

\mbox{\Hypertarget{dispatch_8h_a2915e0e3e21926396b8c15b82d4f6891}\label{dispatch_8h_a2915e0e3e21926396b8c15b82d4f6891}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mmix\_FCMP()}{mmix\_FCMP()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mmix\+\_\+\+FCMP (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structsystem__t}{system\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{sys,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structmmix__processor__t}{mmix\+\_\+processor\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{proc,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structinstr__t}{instr\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{instr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



FCMP \$X, \$Y, \$Z \char`\"{}\+Floating-\/compare\char`\"{}. 

r\mbox{[}\$X\mbox{]} \+:= -\/1 if r\mbox{[}\$Y\mbox{]} $<$ r\mbox{[}\$Z\mbox{]}

r\mbox{[}\$X\mbox{]} \+:= 1 if r\mbox{[}\$Y\mbox{]} $>$ r\mbox{[}\$Z\mbox{]}
